** [#B] AI analysis
*TL;DR:* Large, mostly additive update (v0.9.8.5 -> v0.9.9.5, ~370 commits across v0.9.9/v0.9.9.3/v0.9.9.4/v0.9.9.5); no breaking changes hit the user's config, but optionally bump =gptel-model= to a newer Claude (e.g. =claude-sonnet-4-6= or =claude-opus-4-7=), check whether the new =gptel-tool= =:include= default flipped inline-result behavior of your =read_buffer= / =modify_buffer= tools, and explore the new token usage header-line and pre/post tool-call hooks.

- Your =use-package gptel= block: =gptel-default-mode=, =gptel-api-key=, =gptel-post-response-functions=, =gptel-expert-commands=, =gptel-directives=, =gptel-make-anthropic=, =gptel-context-buffer-mode(-map)= and =gptel-mode-hook= are all still present and unchanged in API. No renames or removals affect you.
- Your =gptel-request= call (=my/gptel-chat-summarize-and-replace=) passes a string prompt with =:stream=, =:system=, =:callback= — still supported. The big =gptel-request= refactor (=cde943d=, =fbc2769=, =358eab4=) split it into a separate library; the public function signature is unchanged. Commit =9ce7c3c= clarifies the prompt-list format but you pass a string, so this is irrelevant.
- *Default OpenAI backend removed* (=4507ff8=, Feb 2026): =gptel-backend=/=gptel-model= default to nil. User explicitly sets both, so no impact here.
- =gptel-make-tool=: commit =46c735c= flipped the default for the =:include= keyword (tool results now included in buffer by default for multi-turn coherence). You set =:include t= explicitly on =read_url=, =emacs_eval=, =emacs_docs=, but rely on the default for =read_buffer= and =modify_buffer= — set =:include t/nil= explicitly on those if you care.
- =9e79e47= changed =gptel-include-reasoning= default to ='ignore= (reasoning visible in buffer but stripped on next turn). You don't set it; positive UX change.
- =gptel-context= API reworked (=5e7d47f=, =445d655=, =734541d=, =0e99125=): new =gptel-context= user option, =gptel--context--alist= marked obsolete, new uniform spec for targeted partial buffer/file context. User only references =gptel-context-buffer-mode= map/hook, not the obsolete variable — no action.
- =b814a27= decoupled =gptel-track-media= from =gptel-context= — user does not set either.
- *Chat buffers persist/restore presets* (=11ddace=, Feb 2026): re-opening saved chats re-applies the recorded preset and warns if missing.
- *In-buffer tool call previews* replace overlay-based confirmation (=69fc610=).
- New preset features: declarative preset composition with =:append=/=:prepend=/=:merge= operators (=3cf7bd0=), built-in =gptel-default= preset to reset configuration (=00e7e12=/=9509af0=) — handy in scripts (=(gptel-with-preset 'gptel-default ...)=), preset modifying backends (=39268e2=). Your =gptel-make-preset 'coding= form still works — different name, no conflict.
- New hooks/features worth knowing about:
  - Token usage display in header line (=4b8894f= + =91150e4=); header-line split into segments (=8a39875=).
  - =gptel-pre-tool-call-functions= / =gptel-post-tool-call-functions= hooks (=61e658b=, =bcb65dc=) — handy given custom tools.
  - Tool call inspection/editing buffer (=7bd4bc9=).
  - =gptel-highlight-mode= via =gptel-highlight-methods= (=2911541=) — margin/fringe/face highlight of LLM responses.
  - Markdown code-block folding (=9d685b9=) and Org/Markdown link validation+annotation (=91ae6fc=, =2d61709=, =83c581d=, =dac4bc0=).
  - MCP synchronous server init (=a24173f=) and MCP tool retrieval fix (=ae97c23=) — relevant for "Set up tool usage via MCP" TODO.
  - =gptel-context= can exclude gitignored files (=514e5f1=).
  - =gptel-rewrite= handles tool calls (=566a1fb=).
  - OpenAI Responses API support (=65d64e6=).

  - Limited Vterm support for =gptel-send= (=d260da8=).
  - GitHub Copilot interactive login (=0975d9c=).

** [#A] AI analysis
*TL;DR:* Big breaking refactor (`ec427c3`) renames bootstrap symbols, struct slots and the installer version — bump `elpaca-installer-version` to `0.12`, rename `elpaca-repos-directory` -> `elpaca-sources-directory` (and its `repos/` path to `sources/`), replace `elpaca--activate-package` with `elpaca-activate` in `elpaca-order`, and replace `(elpaca<-repo-dir pkg)` with `(elpaca<-source-dir pkg)` in `my/elpaca-show-updates`.
- Bootstrap (`Emacs.org` "Install and set up Elpaca" / mirrored in `init.el`, around lines 147-154):
  - `ec427c3 refactor build assumptions` renames `elpaca--activate-package` -> `elpaca-activate`. Your `elpaca-order` currently passes `:build (:not elpaca--activate-package)` — must become `:build (:not elpaca-activate)` or Elpaca will fail to skip activation at bootstrap.
  - Same commit renames struct slot `repo-dir` -> `source-dir`. The on-disk repo dir defcustom is renamed too: `elpaca-repos-directory` is replaced by `elpaca-sources-directory` (no obsolete alias). Your bootstrap defines `elpaca-repos-directory` and `init.el` references it; rename the defvar (and the `repo` binding inside the `let*`) and update the path string from `"repos/"` to `"sources/"` to match the new upstream installer (`doc/installer.el` at `abda553`).
  - Upstream bumped `elpaca-installer-version` from `0.11` to `0.12` in this cycle; the new `elpaca.el` actively `lwarn`'s at startup if your value doesn't match (`elpaca.el:42`: `(or noninteractive (= elpaca-installer-version 0.12) (lwarn ...))`). Bump your `(defvar elpaca-installer-version 0.11)` to `0.12` once the above renames are in.
  - Practical note: switching from `repos/` to `sources/` changes the on-disk layout. Easiest path: do the rename in config, then (per your own cheatsheet) delete `elpaca/` and let Elpaca re-clone everything into `sources/`. The existing builds under `elpaca/builds/` remain valid if you'd prefer to move instead.
- Helpers (`Emacs.org` "Helpers" section, ID `062e8839-654b-4b77-8877-cf4af31ac518`):
  - `my/elpaca-show-updates` calls `(elpaca<-repo-dir pkg)` (line ~280, mirrored in `init.el` line 87). The accessor is gone — change to `(elpaca<-source-dir pkg)`. Without this fix, `my/elpaca-show-updates` will error on the next update cycle. `elpaca<-recipe` and `elpaca--queued` are unchanged and remain usable. (Struct also lost `mono-repo`, gained `declaration`, but you don't reference those.)
- Cheatsheet text on line ~234 mentions `~elpaca/repos/<that-package>~` — update to `elpaca/sources/`. Update instructions in the same section that reference the `repos/` layout are worth a quick scan.
- Public API otherwise stable for what you use:
  - `elpaca`, `elpaca-process-queues`, `elpaca-write-lock-file`, `elpaca-lock-file`, `elpaca-after-init-hook`/`elpaca-after-init-time`, `elpaca-update-menus`, `elpaca-fetch-all`, `elpaca-merge-all`, `elpaca-manager`, `elpaca-generate-autoloads`, `elpaca-use-package-mode`, `elpaca<-recipe` accessor — all still present and behave the same for your usage. `elpaca-write-lock-file` now uses the new generic `elpaca-ref` internally.
  - Bootstrap structure (the surrounding `let*`, `if-let*`, `condition-case`) is identical to the new upstream installer apart from the three renames above.
- New features / behavior changes worth knowing (no action required):
  - `030e723` adds `:on-error` recipe keyword (per-package build-error handler, receives the E struct and error data, non-nil return recovers).
  - `192638f` (tag `v0.1.0`) adds `elpaca-error-functions` top-level recovery hook (first non-nil return suppresses).
  - `:type` recipe keyword is now generic (`ec427c3`); defaults to `git`. New built-in types include `file` (`c08aa86`, `elpaca-file.el`) and `tar` (`608f9e1`, `elpaca-tar.el`) for installing from a local path or tarball.
  - `cf50acf` makes `elpaca-order-functions` / `elpaca-recipe-functions` composable (via `elpaca-run-hook-with-reduce`). You don't set these.
  - `dc6d73e`: `elpaca-menu-item` / `elpaca-recipe` interactive commands now copy paste-ready declarations by default; prefix arg copies raw form.
  - `5aa857a` makes `elpaca--checkout-ref` track the remote branch on checkout — relevant to the documented "detached HEAD" pain in the lock-file workflow (Emacs.org lines ~236-238); worth re-testing whether `elpaca-merge-all` now works after fetching with the lock file disabled.
  - `1e22eb4`, `5543a4f`, `cb981de`, `8ed8347`, `3270e3b`: several mono-repo deadlock and edge-case fixes in the git source backend — pure improvements.
- Removed: `:pre-build` / `:post-build` recipe keywords (per `ec427c3`). Grep shows you don't use them — no impact, but FYI if you copy a recipe from elsewhere.
- Other renames in the refactor (mostly internal, but useful to grep): `elpaca--repo-dirs` -> `elpaca--source-dirs`, `elpaca--link-build-files` -> `elpaca-build-link`, `elpaca--generate-autoloads-async` -> `elpaca-build-autoloads`, `elpaca--byte-compile` -> `elpaca-build-compile`, `elpaca--compile-info` -> `elpaca-build-docs`. None appear in the user's Emacs.org.
- Risks: the three rename fixes are mechanical and low-risk, but must all be applied together before restarting emacs against the new elpaca, or the bootstrap will fail. Recommended order: apply `Emacs.org` edits -> tangle to `init.el` -> only then delete `elpaca/` and restart. The `elpaca.backup/` snapshot you already make is the escape hatch.
- Anchor: last commit `abda553 elpaca-info--recipe: guard against nil E when run interpreted`.

** [#C] AI analysis
*TL;DR:* Nothing strictly to do, but heads-up: =visual-line-fill-column-mode= is now *deprecated* (since 2.7.0) — it still works but emits an obsolescence warning. Our org-present block uses it.
- User's main `(use-package visual-fill-column)` has no customization, no bindings, no hooks; the package itself loads fine.
- Apparent "removal" in a38e3a2 is misleading: the mode is marked obsolete via =(make-obsolete 'visual-line-fill-column-mode ... "2.7.0")= with a README "Deprecating visual-line-fill-column-mode" section. A new autoloaded helper =visual-fill-column-for-vline= is added, intended to be put on =visual-line-mode-hook=.
- 3212ddd: =visual-line-fill-column-mode= now also disables =visual-line-mode= on toggle-off (was previously only =visual-fill-column-mode=) — more symmetric deactivation.
- Our org-present block at =Emacs.org=:1869–1915 calls =(visual-line-fill-column-mode 1)= directly and tracks it in =my/save-modes-state=. It continues to work; expect a byte-compile / obsolescence warning. Optional migrations:
  - Add =(add-hook 'visual-line-mode-hook #'visual-fill-column-for-vline)= and toggle just =visual-line-mode= in the presentation hooks; or
  - Replace =(visual-line-fill-column-mode 1)= with =(visual-line-mode 1)= + =(visual-fill-column-mode 1)= and update the saved mode list.
- New command =visual-fill-column-toggle-center-text= (2.7, 30fc3e4) is available; not used in current config.
- Otherwise: README updates and copyright bump; no API changes affecting the `(use-package visual-fill-column)` at =Emacs.org=:5652.

** [#A] AI analysis
*TL;DR:* Per your own TODO, drop ~:after transient~ from ~(use-package magit ...)~ and remove ~(use-package transient)~ — but only after confirming the bundled transient is new enough (magit still version-asserts transient at load time).
- Your config (Emacs.org line 3436): ~(use-package magit :after transient :defer t :config (general-define-key :keymaps 'magit-diff-section-map "C-<return>" #'magit-diff-visit-worktree-file-other-window))~ plus leader bindings ~gg → magit~, ~gf → magit-file-dispatch~, ~gF → magit-find-file~.
- Action item (your noted TODO): remove the standalone ~(use-package transient)~ block at Emacs.org:3429 and drop ~:after transient~ at line 3437. CAVEAT: magit still enforces a recent transient via runtime asserts — see commits ~569b9656 Add kludge to verify that a recent transient is loaded~ and ~6b10f7f6 Use appropriate signal to verify that a recent transient is loaded~. If your Emacs ships an old transient, magit will signal at load time and you'll need to keep the explicit ~(use-package transient)~. Verify by starting magit after the change; if it errors complaining about transient version, restore the explicit install (you can still drop ~:after transient~ since elpaca already orders deps).
- Span: v4.2.0-54 → v4.5.0+243 (~880 commits). Covers v4.3.0, v4.3.1..v4.3.8, v4.4.0..v4.4.2, v4.5.0, plus heavy post-v4.5.0 development on =main=.
- *Dependency changes (Package-Requires)*:
  - Old: =(emacs "27.1") (compat "30.0.1.0") (dash "2.19.1") (magit-section "4.2.0") (seq "2.24") (transient "0.8.2") (with-editor "3.4.3")=
  - New: =(emacs "28.1") (compat "31.0") (cond-let "0.2") (llama "1.0") (magit-section "4.5") (seq "2.24") (transient "0.13") (with-editor "3.4")=
  - Emacs minimum 27.1 → 28.1 (you're on 30.2, fine).
  - Compat 30 → 31 (shared with jinx/transient updates).
  - *Dropped =dash=* (replaced with =seq= + =##= shorthand from llama).
  - *Added =cond-let=* (~0.2) — Magit author's own package providing =cond-let=, =and$=, =when$= etc.
  - *Added =llama=* (~1.0) — provides =##= anonymous-lambda shorthand (was transitive before).
  - Transient 0.8.2 → 0.13 — headline reason the explicit pin existed.
  - with-editor 3.4.3 → 3.4 (effectively unchanged).
  - Elpaca pulls =cond-let= / =llama= automatically; if recipes are missing, =elpaca-try cond-let= / =elpaca-try llama=.
- Keybinding context unchanged: ~magit-diff-section-map~ and ~magit-diff-visit-worktree-file-other-window~ are not renamed/removed in this range; your ~C-<return>~ binding still works.
- Leader-key targets unchanged: ~magit~, ~magit-file-dispatch~, ~magit-find-file~ are all intact.
- Notable renames in this range (none affect your config, FYI only):
  - ~magit-stage-file~ → ~magit-stage-files~ and ~magit-unstage-file~ → ~magit-unstage-files~ (993cdf0a, Mar 31 2025).
  - ~magit-stage-buffer-file~ / ~magit-unstage-buffer-file~ → ~magit-file-stage~ / ~magit-file-unstage~ (bf920b7f, Mar 31 2025).
  - ~magit-merge-into~ → ~magit-merge-dissolve~ (280fa3dd, Mar 25 2025); merge-menu key changed from =i= to =d=.
  - =magit-section-visibility-indicator= (singular) → =magit-section-visibility-indicators= (plural) (=2d8f43e6=).
  - ~magit-wip-mode~ sub-modes consolidated/removed (a673ca3b, 98ef1070); =magit-wip-after-save-local-mode= and =magit-wip-*-mode-lighter= gone.
  - Many buffer-local vars renamed with obsolete aliases (502f92e7) — backwards compatible.
- Deprecations / removals (none used here):
  - =magit-rev-verify-commit= deprecated in favor of =magit-commit-p= / =magit-commit-oid= (=ac898412=).
  - =magit-find-file-index-noselect= deprecated (=a6aa2359=).
  - =magit-load-config-extensions= removed (=d662ec10=); use =.dir-locals.el=.
  - =magit-section-highlight-hook= replaced with two boolean options (=a53c4024=).
  - Ido support moved out into =magit-ido= (=6aec967e=). You use ivy, unaffected.
- *Behavior changes worth knowing*:
  - =magit-commit= now passes =--verbose= by default (=cbf432d6=, Mar 2026): commit-message buffer includes inline diff (collapsed by default). Unset =--verbose= in the commit transient and save if undesired.
  - Diff syntax highlighting added (=c7b0342d=, Mar 2026): per-file mode highlighting in magit diff buffers, controlled by new =magit-diff-highlight-syntax= (default on).
  - v4.4.0: =RET= now always visits the actual blob; =C-<return>= is the recommended worktree-file binding. New =magit-diff-visit-prefer-worktree= restores old =RET=. You already use =C-<return>= — no impact.
  - =magit-auto-revert-mode= auto-disables when =global-auto-revert-mode= is on (=a48e3176=).
  - =mouse-set-point= remapped in =magit-mode-map= (=fa590662=).
- *New features (optional)*:
  - =magit-revision-jump= bound to =j= in revision mode (=acf71f7e=).
  - =magit-previous-reference= / =magit-next-reference= at =C-c C-r= (=085baa2a=).
  - =git-rebase-drop=, =git-rebase-alter=, =git-rebase-squish= in rebase mode.
  - =magit-format-file-function= and icon prefixes via =all-the-icons= / =nerd-icons= (=223461b5=, =6df061d4=) — could integrate with your nerd-icons setup.
  - New =magit-dired= library with =magit-dired-stage= / =magit-dired-unstage= / =magit-dired-log= (=56197d8a=, =542c2f8a=); available from =magit-file-dispatch= (=C-c M-g=).
  - Shelved branches: date-prefixed; new =magit-wip-purge= / =magit-delete-shelved-branch=.
  - =magit-blame-styles= supports =%h= for truncated hashes (=2dd886c2=).
  - Blob navigation aware of index blobs; Octopus-merge support via =magit-merge-{plain,editmsg,nocommit}=.
  - =magit-branch-name-suggestions= option.
  - New Lisp hooks invoked from Git hooks: =magit-common-git-post-commit-functions=, =magit-git-post-{commit,merge,rewrite}-functions=, =magit-{before-change,after-apply}-functions=.
  - New face =magit-diff-conflict-heading-highlight=.
  - =magit-process-yes-or-no-prompt-regexp= and password-prompt regexps reworked to better detect CLI passphrase prompts.
  - =magit-toggle-profiling= / =magit-toggle-subprocess-record= (already in your locked snapshot) for diagnosing slowness.
- Forge note: your commented-out forge block (Emacs.org:3468) can now be considered again — the magit/transient rework is the historical blocker you mentioned; revisit if desired (not required by this update).
- Risk level [#A] mainly because of the two new transitive deps (=cond-let=, =llama=), the Emacs minimum bump, the =--verbose= default flip on =magit-commit=, and the transient-pin question your own TODO calls out.

** [#B] AI analysis
*TL;DR:* Nothing required; optionally revisit your own TODO about whether ~(use-package transient)~ is still needed now that magit is also being updated.
- Your Emacs.org only has a bare ~(use-package transient)~ with no ~:custom~, ~:config~, ~:bind~ or any references to transient symbols — you installed it solely as a version override for magit. So none of the renames/removals below affect your config.
- Span: v0.8.3 → v0.13.3 (covers 0.8.4–0.8.8, 0.9.x, 0.10.0, 0.10.1, 0.11.0, 0.12.0, 0.13.x).
- Across this range there are no breaking changes that touch user-facing symbols you actually use. Notable items, listed only for awareness:
  - ~d361d27~ (Oct 14 2025) "Require Emacs 28.1" — bumped minimum Emacs version (fine if you're on >= 28.1).
  - compat dependency bumped twice (Apr 2025, May 2025) and moved to =compat-31= (=30e45ed=). Elpaca shares it.
  - ~88ff8d6~ "transient-hide-during-minibuffer-read: Remove obsolete variable" — removed obsolete defcustom (you don't set it).
  - ~1c138dc~ "transient-show-menu: Renamed option" and ~e5a4c9a~ "transient-enable-menu-navigation: Renamed option" — renamed defcustoms (you don't set them).
  - =c4e0cba= (May 16 2025) "Stricter key binding format": all key bindings must now be specified as key descriptions. Internal to how prefixes are defined — affects magit (a consumer), not you.
  - =transient-get-value= replaced with three functions (only affects code that calls it directly).
  - Quit-inhibit while menu is active (0.9.0); =Cond-Let= adoption; native-compiled Lisp advising; text-conversion suspension while transient active; isearch-resume handling.
  - Many new opt-in options added (e.g. ~transient-prefer-reading-value~, ~transient-use-accessible-formats~ / ~-values~, ~transient-describe-menu~, ~transient-select-menu-window~, ~transient-common-command-prefix~, ~transient-error-on-insert-failure~, ~transient-post-exit-hook~, ~transient-navigate-to-group-descriptions~) — none default-on in a way that requires action.
  - *API additions*: =transient-scope= got a =CLASSES= argument; advising suffix commands now supported; new =transient-cons-option= class; =transient-buttonize=, =transient-get-summary=, =transient-object= base class, recursion shorthand, mouse menu navigation. All additive.
- Action item from your own TODO at the top of the file: since magit is being updated alongside transient, this is the natural moment to test whether magit still requires the pinned ~transient~ override. If magit works without it, you can drop both ~(use-package transient)~ and the ~:after transient~ in the magit block (see Emacs.org around the "Magit" section). With this transient bump alone you don't have to change anything; the corresponding magit update is the right place to revisit the workaround.

** [#B] AI analysis
*TL;DR:* Major release 9.7.20 → 9.8.4 (740+ commits). The "inline images" subsystem has been generalized into a "link previews" subsystem, and three symbols the user *does* use have been renamed (old names still work as obsolete aliases, so nothing breaks today, but should be updated to avoid future breakage and obsolete warnings).
- Major version bump to Org 9.8 (=8280cf05a=, tag =release_9.8=, =aec0f836c= "Bump minimal Emacs version"). Development is now 10.0-pre (=dc69efb2c=).

** Breaking changes / renames that touch user's config
- ~org-startup-with-inline-images~ → ~org-startup-with-link-previews~. Behaviour unchanged for image links; the new var also applies to other previewable link types (not configured here). Action: rename in the ~setq-default~ at ~Emacs.org:1485~.
- ~org-display-inline-images~ → ~org-link-preview-region~. Used at ~Emacs.org:1902~ inside ~my/on-presentation-start~. Old name still works (obsolete).
- ~org-remove-inline-images~ → ~org-link-preview-clear~. Used at ~Emacs.org:1925~ inside ~my/on-presentation-quit~. Old name still works (obsolete).
- ~org-toggle-inline-images~ command (=C-c C-x C-v=) is replaced by ~org-link-preview~ with different prefix-arg semantics (region/at-point/entry instead of whole-buffer toggle). User does not rebind this key, so impact is just a UX shift. To restore old behavior:
  #+begin_src emacs-lisp
  (eval-after-load 'org-keys
    (org-defkey org-mode-map (kbd "C-c C-x C-v") #'org-toggle-inline-images))
  #+end_src

** Other renames/obsoletes — none used in =Emacs.org=
- =5501a0f80= renamed =org-edit-src-content-indentation= → =org-src-content-indentation= (not set by user).
- =40fabc07b= removed obsolete =org-let=/=org-let2= (not used).
- =5eb0d860e= obsoleted =org-show-empty-lines-in-parent= (not used).
- =9ccf56b3c= obsoleted =org-advertized-archive-subtree= (not used).
- =d198e689c= "Remove deprecated show command" (not used).
- Deprecated hooks/functions =org-show-context(-detail)= (=ffccdb629=), =org-export-before-parsing-hook= (=1267b81ec=), =org-export-before-processing-hook= (=de998dfe8=), =org-store-link-props= (=c8dcd11e3=) — not used.
- ~org-cycle-display-inline-images~ → ~org-cycle-display-link-previews~ (not used).
- ~org-cycle-inline-images-display~ → ~org-cycle-link-previews-display~ (not used).

** Other 9.8 behavioural changes — do not affect this config
- Diary-style timestamps now treated as ~active~ for export (~org-export-with-timestamps~ / ~org-icalendar-with-timestamps~). New value ~active-exclude-diary~ restores old behavior. User does not set these, so default =t= effectively unchanged. iCal export will include diary stamps by default; fine.
- ~ob-calc~ now formats vectors/matrices as Org tables by default. Not used.
- ~org-resource-download-policy~ ~ask~ now errors out (instead of silently skipping) in batch mode for unsafe remote =#+include:=. Only relevant for batch publishing scripts.
- Default ~org-babel-latex-process-alist~ no longer pulls from ~org-preview-latex-process-alist~ (uses latexmk/latex). User doesn't customize either.
- New ~:tree-type~ subsets of ~(year quarter month week day)~ (plus function form) for datetree captures. User's ~file+olp+datetree~ entries (=Emacs.org:2586=) use default which still maps to =(year month day)= — unchanged.
- New ~org-edit-keep-region~ option (region kept after structure edits since 9.7). Not customized.
- Minor protocol/bookmarklet changes for ~org-protocol~; user does not appear to use it.

** User's symbols verified still valid
=org-export-backends=, =org-modules= (with =org-habit=, =org-inlinetask=), =org-startup-*=, =org-pretty-entities=, =org-use-sub-superscripts=, =org-ellipsis=, =org-log-into-drawer=, =org-id-link-to-org-use-id=, =org-habit-graph-column=, =org-priority-faces=, =org-todo-keyword-faces=, =org-structure-template-alist=, =org-babel-load-languages=, =org-confirm-babel-evaluate=, =org-agenda-scheduled-leaders=/=-deadline-leaders=/=-block-separator=/=-prefix-format=/=-sorting-strategy=, =org-priority-down/up= — all unaffected.

** Useful non-breaking improvements (optional, commit refs)
- Numeric priorities supported across the codebase (=4faa300eb=, =5a1cc9224=, =b19fc7b3b=, =aa4cd87d8=); user's =org-priority-faces= keyed on chars ?A/?B/?C still works as before.
- ~7660d40c9~ =org-yank-image-save-method= can now be a function (user currently uses =org-download=).
- ~b02c34948~ =org-tags-sort-function= may now be a list of functions; =23d219693= adds tag-hierarchy sorting.
- ~977f0ff132~ / =77f0ff132= =org-support-shift-select= can force shift-select on timestamps.
- ~004e0828b~ new =org-latex-descriptive-environment= for LaTeX export.
- ~972d5c2ba~ Org now queries before overwriting existing attachment/DnD/yank files — purely additive prompt.
- ~62a5910d8~ new =org-archive-finalize-hook=; ~9f3ee0fa5~ =org-archive-save-context-info= can save parent ID.
- New generic link-preview API (=:preview= in =org-link-parameters=); user may want to use =org-link-preview-region= / =org-link-preview-clear= in =org-present= helpers.
- ~repeat-mode~ navigation: =C-c C-n/p/f/b/u= and block/link nav repeatable via new keymaps =org-navigation-repeat-map=, =org-link-navigation-repeat-map=, =org-block-navigation-repeat-map= — kicks in only when =repeat-mode= is enabled.
- ~org-persist~ performance/correctness fixes (=38cd9b0a3=, =ab7df301d=).
- ~org-fold~ regression fixes (=04e0e67b3=, =92e165162=, =1a3564ada=).
- Many ~ox-html~/~ox-latex~/~ox-odt~/~ox-texinfo~ improvements (mostly not relevant; user's export list is ='(ascii html icalendar latex odt md)=).

** Recommended edits to =Emacs.org=
1. Line 1485: ~org-startup-with-inline-images t~ → ~org-startup-with-link-previews t~.
2. Line 1902: ~(org-display-inline-images)~ → ~(org-link-preview-region nil nil (point-min) (point-max))~ (or keep as-is, still works).
3. Line 1925: ~(org-remove-inline-images)~ → ~(org-link-preview-clear)~ (or keep as-is).

If minimum churn is preferred, only edit (1) is strictly necessary right now — (2) and (3) just suppress future obsolete warnings.

** [#B] AI analysis
*TL;DR:* Major 9.0.0 → 10.0.0 release (~240 commits, year+ of changes); nothing required, but this is a big jump. All options you set in ~(use-package lsp-mode ...)~ still exist with the same semantics. One thing worth checking: =377662d014= overhauled the =lsp-face-semhl-*= family for LSP 3.17 — if you ever enable semantic tokens for Haskell (you remap =lsp-face-semhl-operator= and =lsp-face-semhl-method= in =my/lsp-haskell-local-face-setup= and set =lsp-haskell-plugin-semantic-tokens-global-on t=), verify the remaps still resolve. Optionally consider new ~lsp-format-buffer-on-save~ and ~lsp-fix-all~ features.

- Major release (tag ~10.0.0~, commit ~913a6c07f1~). Drops Emacs 27 (~ac71048270~) and 28 (~5d9e72816a~) — irrelevant on Emacs 30+.
- All used options still exist: ~lsp-use-plists~, ~lsp-modeline-diagnostics-enable~, ~lsp-modeline-diagnostics-scope~, ~lsp-modeline-code-actions-enable~, ~lsp-eldoc-enable-hover~, ~lsp-eldoc-render-all~, ~lsp-headerline-breadcrumb-enable~, ~lsp-headerline-breadcrumb-segments~, ~lsp-imenu-sort-methods~, ~lsp-file-watch-ignored-directories~. The ~LSP_USE_PLISTS~ env var and ~lsp-enable-which-key-integration~ hook are unchanged. Faces =lsp-inlay-hint-face= and =lsp-details-face= still exist (used in =my/on-theme-enabled= advice). =lsp-command-map= (used for the ~,~ keybinding) unchanged.

*** Breaking-ish changes (potentially relevant)
- *lsp-interface pcase forms* (~b8e9e999e1~, called out in CHANGELOG as "*This is a breaking change.* (See #4430)"): per-interface ~(INTERFACE ...)~ pcase forms are no longer generated; code must use ~(lsp-interface INTERFACE ...)~. =Emacs.org= does not pcase against lsp-interface types — unaffected, but third-party packages depending on lsp-mode could be affected (watch for runtime errors).
- *Semantic tokens overhaul* (~377662d014~): =lsp-face-semhl-*= family reworked for LSP 3.17 (new faces like =lsp-face-semhl-enum-member=, =modifier=, =decorator=). User has =face-remap-add-relative= for =lsp-face-semhl-operator= → =lsp-face-semhl-keyword= (Emacs.org:4566; note pre-existing typo =:foregrund=) and =lsp-face-semhl-method= → =lsp-face-semhl-function= (Emacs.org:4568), plus =lsp-haskell-plugin-semantic-tokens-global-on t= (line 4616). Faces are common LSP 3.17 token types so should still exist, but inheritance defaults may have changed — open a Haskell buffer post-update and confirm operator/method recoloring. Companion fix ~0c3481b2ec~ resolves duplicate defface definitions; ~de584ae57b~ switches semantic tokens to =font-lock-keywords= (transparent).
- *Ruff client rename*: =ruff-lsp= → =ruff= (vars renamed, command changed to ~["ruff" "server"]~). Not used in config.

*** Plist-mode improvements (user sets ~lsp-use-plists t~)
- ~9323ce94d3~ gopls inlay hints, ~514e256ab2~ gopls code lenses, ~f752629ded~ code-actions diagnostics location, ~7c5b52638f~ preserve empty-object capabilities, ~fbc926fd31~ classify JSON-RPC messages by method before id — all bug fixes for the plist path. No action needed.

*** Breadcrumb-related
- ~74e82c3b7f~ makes ~lsp-headerline--check-breadcrumb~ public for ~after-*-jump-hooks~ wiring; ~e21f0d2f75~ fixes a nil-location crash. Both improvements to a feature you use.

*** Other internals
- ~d3110e3d7d~ switches overlay-keymap handling to a transient map. Your ~(general-define-key :keymaps 'lsp-mode-map "," lsp-command-map)~ still works through ~lsp-mode-map~ — no change required.
- ~ca79027f47~ replaces =url-copy-file= thread with =make-process curl= in =lsp-download-install= — internal.
- Several =perf:= commits reducing allocations in file-watch hot paths.

*** Optional new features
- ~1fb656e4e5~ + ~57e30610cd~ + ~d35aa757a3~: ~lsp-format-buffer-on-save~ defcustom, settable via ~.dir-locals.el~. User currently wires =lsp-format-buffer= into =before-save-hook= manually in =my/haskell-mode-setup= (Emacs.org:4582) — could optionally migrate to ~(lsp-format-buffer-on-save t)~ in ~:custom~. There's also a related ~lsp-fix-all-on-save~ option.
- ~69b08f25d3~: new ~lsp-fix-all~ command for buffer-wide ~source.fixAll~ code actions; discoverable via which-key under your ~,~ prefix.
- ~503fd0fff1~: LSP 3.17 ~positionEncoding~ negotiation — invisible improvement.
- Pull diagnostics (basic LSP 3.17 support).
- ~7a1e1fb60e~ =workspace/willRenameFiles= / =didRenameFiles= via =vc-git-rename-file= advice — files renamed via VC will now notify the LS.
- ~883dded91e~ JSON validation explicitly enabled by default — non-issue normally; if you see new JSON diagnostics, that's why.
- Many new language clients (LTEX+, swift-ts, MATLAB, typespec-ts, c3, Postgres LS, tombi/TOML, odin/ols, Tinymist/typst, ron, deno install, biome, fish-lsp, just-lsp, wasm-language-tools, crates-lsp, tsgo, perl-ts, fortitude, Python ty, neocaml, fsharp-ts, etc.) — additive only.

*** Dir-local
- The =safe-local-variable-values= block in =Emacs.org= (line ~5770) that adds to =lsp-file-watch-ignored-directories= via =with-eval-after-load= still works — variable and load behavior unchanged.

*** Action
- Accept update, then open a Haskell buffer (HLS running, semantic tokens active) and confirm operator/method recoloring in =my/lsp-haskell-local-face-setup= still works.
- Optional: migrate manual =before-save-hook= wiring of =lsp-format-buffer= in =my/haskell-mode-setup= to the new =lsp-format-buffer-on-save= custom.

** [#A] AI analysis
*TL;DR:* Rename =sideline-flycheck-success= face to =sideline-flycheck-info= in your =use-package sideline-flycheck= block — upstream renamed the face (breaking change, in 0.2.0). Also: new per-level prefix customs that resolve your existing TODO.
- Breaking: commit =8602950 feat: Rename success face to info face= renamed the defface =sideline-flycheck-success= to =sideline-flycheck-info=; the internal backend =cond= dispatch was updated to reference the new face for info-level diagnostics. Your =:config= calls =(set-face-attribute 'sideline-flycheck-success nil ...)= inside =my/on-theme-enabled= will either become a silent no-op (face auto-created but no longer used by the backend) or raise an =Invalid face= error on theme load — either way it stops affecting display. Update it to =sideline-flycheck-info=.
- Bonus: commit =dc76769 feat: Add prefix for levels= adds the customs =sideline-flycheck-error-prefix=, =sideline-flycheck-warning-prefix=, =sideline-flycheck-info-prefix= (defaults ="="=, concatenated to the message before display). Internal level dispatch was rewritten via =pcase= over a new =sideline-flycheck--get-level= helper. This directly satisfies your TODO comment at =Emacs.org= line 4131 "Somehow define following prefixes ✖ ⓘ ⚠ for errors / warning / success?" — set them via =:custom=, e.g. =(sideline-flycheck-error-prefix "✖ ")=, =(sideline-flycheck-warning-prefix "⚠ ")=, =(sideline-flycheck-info-prefix "ⓘ ")=, and drop the TODO.

** [#B] AI analysis
*TL;DR:* Nothing required; optionally note the cache-file rename, the new transient-by-default cache, the ~projectile-auto-discover~ default flip, and the soft-deprecation of prefix-less ~.projectile~ entries mentioned in your cheatsheet.
- Span: v2.8.0-48 → v2.9.1-177 (~177 commits past v2.9.1 plus v2.9.0/v2.9.1 itself; heavy bug-fix / perf / TRAMP-correctness round).
- User config is minimal and untouched by this update: ~projectile-switch-project-action~ ('projectile-dired'), ~:bind-keymap "C-c p"~, ~projectile-completion-system 'ivy~, ~(projectile-mode)~ — all still supported. ~projectile-completion-system~ remains; `ivy` is still a valid value. Inline =(projectile-project-root)= (line 4075) and the =counsel-projectile-rg-region-or-symbol= wrapper using =projectile-symbol-or-selection-at-point= still work.
- *Dependency changes*: old =(emacs "25.1")= → new =(emacs "27.1") (compat "30")=. Emacs min 25.1 → 27.1 (you're on 30.2). New =compat= dep — shared with jinx/magit updates so elpaca pulls it once.
- Cache file renamed from ~.projectile.cache~ to ~.projectile-cache.eld~ (81a7e5d). If you globally gitignore the old name, you may want to add the new one (commit 2793900 adds it to projectile's own .gitignore). Old =~/.emacs.d/projectile.cache= becomes an orphan you can delete at leisure.
- Cache is now *transient by default* (a4a6cac); persistent caching must be opted in via =(projectile-enable-caching 'persistent)= or =t=. Side effects: no empty cache files on disk (cdb22f6, ce6e637). =projectile-cache-current-file= now uses an idle timer (0efac68, 28014da) — coalesced flushes.
- ~projectile-auto-discover~ default flipped from t to nil (4dd84b0). Auto project discovery is now opt-in. You don't set this var, so behavior change is "fewer surprise scans on startup".
- New common prefix for project-lifecycle commands (=dd1a8e2=): add/remove/cleanup-known-project keys inside =projectile-command-map= reshuffled under a common prefix. Everyday bindings (=p=, =f=, =d=, =b=, =s s/r/g=) unchanged — only muscle memory for lifecycle keys. Use =C-c p C-h= to relearn.
- Mode-line update path changed: now via =window-configuration-change-hook= so non-file buffers like magit get the right project info (#1823).
- New commands/features you might find useful (no action needed):
  - ~projectile-find-file-all~ (0285927): find files ignoring VCS rules.
  - ~projectile-discard-root-cache~ (66b54e9): clear root cache.
  - ~projectile-add-known-project~ keybind (=A=) added in ~projectile-command-map~ (55db082) — reachable via your ~C-c p~ prefix.
  - ~projectile-global-ignore-file-patterns~ (cc85811).
  - ~projectile-auto-cleanup-known-projects~ (e6c0f5f).
  - =projectile-max-file-buffer-count= (now documented).
  - eat terminal support (6bc4e81), swift project type (09e8191), jujutsu vcs (4e1cfd5).
- Better integration with built-in ~project.el~: ~project-projectile~ now autoloaded (9dd005e), ~project-name~/~project-buffers~ implemented (4ad624e), plus new "Migrating from project.el" docs (957d808). No impact unless you mix the two.
- *Cheatsheet note (line 3362 in Emacs.org):* your cheatsheet says "add .projectile file to the project root to explicitly mark it as a project". The dirconfig format had a soft-deprecation of *prefix-less entries* (6be2d06) and a stricter parser (4928cbf, 2b49c82). The empty-file-as-marker usage you describe still works; only the contents grammar tightened. No edit required, but if you ever add lines to such a file, prefix them (~+~/~-~/~!~). Optional silencers: =projectile-warn-on-prefixless-dirconfig-lines=, =projectile-warn-when-dirconfig-is-ignored=.
- Internal: =cl-lib= largely replaced with =seq.el= and =alist-get=; =projectile-find-references= now uses public =xref-show-xrefs=; fallback for missing tag is =xref-find-definitions= instead of removed =find-tag=. Invisible.
- Many performance fixes (rounds 1–4: 5d87663, 97fa0b8, 4469d33, 0cdd2a9) and TRAMP improvements (40156ca and the 06:51 cluster on Apr 29) — silent wins.
- Bug fixes touching =projectile-replace=, =projectile-find-dir=, =projectile-root-top-down=, grep with special chars, replace-regexp on missing files, mode-line in non-file buffers, etc. All upside.
- Counsel-projectile note: separate package, unaffected — it relies on =projectile-completing-read= and other untouched public APIs.
- Suggested post-update: optionally run =projectile-discard-root-cache= once (or restart Emacs).

** [#A] AI analysis
*TL;DR:* Likely no action required, but verify =elfeed-db-directory= behavior — commit =33d6fd8= changes the default to ~/.config/emacs/elfeed for *new* users while preserving an existing =~/.elfeed/= if present. If you want to be safe (or migrate), pin it explicitly.
- *Default change clarified* (=33d6fd8= "Use ~/.config/emacs/elfeed as Elfeed directory by default"): the commit message states "only affects new users. If the setting has not been customized and an old =~/.elfeed= directory is present, Elfeed will continue to use it." So if you already have =~/.elfeed/= populated, your DB keeps working untouched. If unsure, run =ls ~/.elfeed=; if present, no migration needed. If you want a hard guarantee, add ~(setq elfeed-db-directory "~/.elfeed")~ in the ~:config~ block, or move =~/.elfeed= → =~/.config/emacs/elfeed= before first run.
- Span: ~216 commits since locked =a39fb78= (3.4.2). No new release tag. The repo has moved from =skeeto/elfeed= to =emacs-elfeed/elfeed= (new maintainer team — Daniel Mendler is now driving it, hence the consistent linting/refactoring burst). =NEWS.md= has *not* been updated for this batch, so analysis is from the commit log + repo inspection. Elpaca's recipe (likely MELPA) is expected to follow; the lock-file delta already shows the new origin. =elfeed-web= was split out into =emacs-elfeed/elfeed-web= (=643e09c=) — you don't use it.
- New minimum requirements: Emacs 27.1 (=bde19ca=) and Compat 31 (=782c9a0=). Elpaca pulls compat; verify the compat entry in this same update log applies cleanly.
- *Database upgrade functionality removed* (=450615b=): the auto-upgrade path from 2018 (Emacs 25 → 26 index format) is gone. Only relevant for an ancient =~/.elfeed/index= from pre-Emacs-26 — virtually certainly not your case.
- =4e83cca= renamed ~elfeed-sort-order~ → ~elfeed-search-sort-order~; old name kept as obsolete alias (not used here).
- =2cb8f8c= / =a73ddeb= mark ~elfeed-show-mode~ / ~elfeed-search-mode~ non-interactive and add =(modes ...)= declarations so =elfeed-show-*= / =elfeed-search-*= commands are hidden from =M-x= outside their buffers. Modes also refactored to =define-derived-mode= and now set =revert-buffer-function=. Cleaner =M-x= completion; no breakage.
- New entry-point: =M-x elfeed= now calls =elfeed-entry-point= (=3889251=, defaults to =elfeed-search=); new commands =elfeed-search= and =elfeed-tree=. =M-x elfeed= continues to work as before by default.
- *=*elfeed-log*= buffer now ephemeral by default* (=4b5da2d=) — created lazily, killed when empty. Not user-visible.
- *Obsoleted (none used here)*: =elfeed-expose=, =elfeed-kill-buffer=, =elfeed-get-url-at-point=, =elfeed-strip-properties=, =elfeed-search-quit-window=, =elfeed-search-update--force= (kept as alias). Internal rename =with-elfeed-db-visit= → =elfeed-db-visit= (=021344a=).
- *Nice new features available but optional*:
  - ~elfeed-tree-mode~ (=072a609=); ~elfeed-delete-feed~ (=b2b8320=) / =elfeed-db-delete=.
  - ~elfeed-confirm-browse-url~ (=7242a7e=); secondary browse-url bindings (=73ba2c0=) — =B= for browse-url-secondary, =elfeed-search-browse-url-secondary=, =elfeed-show-visit-secondary=.
  - =elfeed-search-set-entry-title= / =elfeed-search-set-feed-title= bound to =t= / =T= in search.
  - completing-read for prompts/tags (=8b6f058=, =28dad74=); =elfeed-search-completion= (with =completing-read-multiple=, opt-out available).
  - Mouse support in search (=3d66d7a=); =elfeed-search/show-mode-menu= (menu bar); bookmark handler types; custom faces for show buffer (=elfeed-entry= faces).
  - Shorter age filters like ~@6months~ (=4b4840f=).
  - Other new defcustoms: =elfeed-use-libxml=, =elfeed-default-directory=, =elfeed-search-update-delay= (debounce), =elfeed-entry-point=.
- Anchor: last commit =7a47724 Indentation=.

** [#C] AI analysis
*TL;DR:* Nothing to do.
- Update is 0.14.2 → 0.15.1 + post-release master; almost all commits are bugfixes or internal refactors / copyright bumps. Lazy-loading refactor (=33b82a0=) gives a measurable startup win (ivy ~50 ms → ~13 ms; counsel ~180 ms → ~80 ms).
- User config sets only documented customs (~ivy-height~, ~ivy-use-virtual-buffers~, ~ivy-display-style~, ~ivy-count-format~, ~ivy-extra-directories~, ~ivy-format-functions-alist~ with ~ivy-format-function-arrow-line~, ~ivy-re-builders-alist~ with ~ivy--regex-ignore-order~, ~ivy-initial-inputs-alist~) plus evil keybindings on ~ivy-minibuffer-map~ / ~ivy-switch-buffer-map~ / ~ivy-reverse-i-search-map~ to ~ivy-next-line~ / ~ivy-previous-line~ / ~ivy-alt-done~ / ~ivy-done~ / ~ivy-backward-kill-word~ / ~ivy-switch-buffer-kill~ / ~ivy-reverse-i-search-kill~, then enables ~ivy-mode~ — none of these symbols are renamed, removed, or have semantics altered by the new commits.
- Specific bug fixes worth noting:
  - =576f421=, =05f1d82=, =5e93415=, =5a041b1=, =a0b2150= — =ivy-completion-in-region= return value, point placement on exact completion, sole match exit, base-size handling.
  - =10b544f= fix 1/0 =ivy-count-format= for zero candidates — strict improvement for your =(ivy-count-format "(%d/%d) ")=.
  - =2c64b29= fix minibuffer hooks lifecycle.
  - =4b1df7c= + =ec94213= prompt text-property fixes (don't replace, fix =(confirm)= / =(match required)= faces).
  - =fd4f157= fix =M-x= completion-predicate filtering; also marks =ivy-define-key= obsolete (you don't call it — your evil-define-key on ivy maps is unaffected).
- =33b82a0= ("Try to load libraries more lazily") and =4defb81= ("Directly require cl-lib") rearrange internal requires but should be transparent to consumers; =c9cdd22= "Only enable dynamic exhibit delay while typing" tweaks a perf default, no config change needed.
- =7c4fa07= ports to Emacs 31's ~completing-read-multiple~ (detects =crm=, falls back to =completing-read-default=) and =1005bff= resignals errors preserving eq-uality in Emacs 31 — only relevant if/when upgrading Emacs. Also an Emacs 28.1 minimum bump in this range.

- yaml-ts-mode shift-width tweaks landed and were reverted (=092408d=); net-zero.

- Risk: vertico ~gg~/~G~ and magit ~M-j~/~M-k~ are the only added bindings that could shadow user customizations — user has none for those keys in those maps.

** [#C] AI analysis
*TL;DR:* Nothing to do; safe routine update. v4.1.0-136 -> v4.2.1-97 (~120 commits across ~14 months).
- User config only sets `doom-modeline-height` (40), `doom-modeline-buffer-encoding` (nil), `doom-modeline-minor-modes` (nil), and calls `(doom-modeline-mode 1)` — a very small surface area.
- `f6fb1f6` "change default value of `doom-modeline-height'" (Jul 12 2025; from `(+ (frame-char-height) 4)` to `(+ (window-font-height nil 'mode-line) 4)`) is irrelevant: the user sets the value explicitly.
- No commit renames, removes, or changes semantics of any of the four symbols used. `doom-modeline-buffer-encoding` and `doom-modeline-minor-modes` still accept the same nil value.
- Remaining changes are new opt-in features (selection info segment `0a420cf`, worktree indicator `fcf602b`, dedicated-window flag `ec27cdb`, tree-sitter indentation `a150d53`, unicode window numbers `c884489`, VCS-state -> face alist `75dc662`, speedbar support `9a3631c`, mu4e/IRC/reader/pdf segments, modal-state display `14cade0`, `doom-modeline-add-segment` / `doom-modeline-remove-segment` `593c3d5`/`bcf8cc0`, configurable remote-host display `f2f049c`, tab-bar-format-global alternative `83abca3`, buffer-position control `ddc2d47`) — all default off or backwards-compatible.
- Perf/refactors (modals segment caching `005907e`, font-height caching `c599095`, region-update optimization `e425971`, focus/window handling simplifications, right-alignment logic `abb1b4e`), Emacs 30.1/30.2/31 compiler warning fixes — no minimum-version bump.
- Many bug fixes: flycheck/flymake state validation, battery edge cases, frame focus delay, child-frame active-modeline, TRAMP hang in git worktree detection (`b6ce0ba`), mu4e segment, pdf-tools page number in continuous-scroll, git-timemachine display, face inheritance, meow eager loading (`85dc5f0`).

** [#B] AI analysis
*TL;DR:* Nothing required; large jump from 34.1 to 36.0 (crosses =6e43c07e= v35.0 and =ebddfd89= v36.0) brings minor behavior tweaks but the symbols you use (=global-flycheck-mode=, =flycheck-display-errors-delay=, =flycheck-next-error=/=previous-error=/=list-errors=, =flycheck-overlay-errors-at=) are unchanged.
- None of your configured options or commands were renamed/removed.
- Behavior changes that may be visible at runtime (no config action needed):
  - =95f40340= "Include info-level errors in mode-line indicator" — mode-line counter may now show info entries you didn't see before; mode-line indicator is also now colored and uses the format =errors|warnings|infos=. New =flycheck-mode-success-indicator= defcustom.
  - =4615773d= "Strictly enforce flycheck-navigation-minimum-level" — affects =flycheck-next-error=/=flycheck-previous-error= jumps; default level is unchanged, but stricter now.
  - =37b046cd= "Exclude error messages buffer from global-flycheck-mode" — your =(global-flycheck-mode)= no longer activates in =*Messages*=-like buffers (a fix, not a regression).
  - =1c8af1b6= "Re-check buffer after revert" — buffers you revert (e.g. via =global-auto-revert-mode=) will be re-linted automatically.
  - =ddca9f77= "Isolate bidi characters in error message snippets" + =596fa68e= "Force C locale for checker processes" — safer/more consistent checker output (en_US locale, so neutral for you).
- Security: =77c100c3= "Mitigate CVE-2024-53920 in emacs-lisp checker subprocess" — relevant since you run =global-flycheck-mode= in Elisp buffers.
- Many obsolete checkers removed (16 total): =javascript-jshint=, =scss/sass= (Ruby Sass), =sass-lint=, =scss-lint=, =json-jsonlint=, =asciidoc=, =css-csslint=, =coffee-coffeelint=, =typescript-tslint=, =yaml-ruby=, =ruby-jruby=, =eruby-erubis=/=ruumba=, =protobuf-prototool=, =nix-linter=, =xml-xmlstarlet=. You don't reference any of these. Stylelint <14 support also dropped (breaking in 35.0) — doesn't affect you.
- Misc relevant additions you may find useful (no action required): =5f661852= =javascript-oxlint= checker, =367551e6= =org-lint= checker for Org files, =5840540e= =markdown-markdownlint-cli2=, =3df4440f= =flycheck-error-list-after-jump-hook=, =1e21055f= allow =flycheck-command-map= as prefix command, =salt-lint=, =perl-perlimports=, =r= (builtin parse), new shellcheck options (=flycheck-shellcheck-args=, =flycheck-shellcheck-enabled-checks=, =flycheck-shellcheck-infer-shell=), pyright rule names captured as error IDs, error explainer for =python-ruff=.
- *Watch-out*: the new =org-lint= checker will silently start running on Org buffers with =global-flycheck-mode= on — could spam diagnostics in =Emacs.org= itself. If that happens, suppress via =flycheck-disabled-checkers=.
- =flycheck-posframe= and =flycheck-inline= integration: the helpers you call (=flycheck-overlay-errors-at=, =flycheck-display-errors-function=, =flycheck-posframe-show-posframe=) are untouched.

** [#B] AI analysis
*TL;DR:* Nothing required; optionally adopt =vterm-toggle-togglable-buffer-functions= to make =my/vterm-toggle-list-other-buffers= robust against the new buffer-list semantics — especially useful to exclude =*claude*= buffers from rotation.
- =dae4ae5= "Don't update =vterm-toggle--buffer-list= when not toggled": user code reads =vterm-toggle--buffer-list= directly in =my/vterm-toggle-list-other-buffers=. Previously every =vterm-mode= buffer got added; now only buffers created via the toggle path are added. If user ever spawns vterm buffers outside =vterm-toggle= (e.g. =M-x vterm=, =my/vterm-new=), they will no longer appear in the modeline list. Likely fine since user's flow goes through =vterm-toggle=, but worth noting.
- =6fff527= / =0c29359= add =vterm-toggle-togglable-buffer-functions= defcustom (PR #43) and =vterm-toggle-togglable-buffer-p=; all internal =derived-mode-p 'vterm-mode= / =eq major-mode 'vterm-mode= checks are replaced. Default empty list ⇒ unchanged behavior. Since claude-code runs inside vterm buffers named like =*claude*=, a predicate could keep =,n=/=,p= cycling and =my/vterm-toggle-modeline-buffers-list= away from those:
  #+begin_src emacs-lisp
    (add-to-list 'vterm-toggle-togglable-buffer-functions
                 (lambda (buf)
                   (not (string-prefix-p "*claude" (buffer-name buf)))))
  #+end_src
- =81d031f= (PR #44) only triggers the togglable check inside =vterm-mode-hook= — interacts with user's =add-hook 'vterm-mode-hook #'my/vterm-toggle-setup-modeline=, but the hook just appends to =mode-line-misc-info=, no conflict.
- =15112d2= removes stray =(require 'vterm)= — no impact (vterm functions already =declare-function='d, user has =vterm= configured separately).
- =80989c6= (PR #45) merge commit only; no behavioural change visible from log.

** [#B] AI analysis
*TL;DR:* Nothing required; optionally consider project-local reference revisions to address the very concern in your own config NOTE.
- Your config uses =diff-hl-set-reference-rev= / =diff-hl-reset-reference-rev= with a NOTE warning that it sets the ref-rev /globally/ and causes "weird behaviour" across projects. Commit =a31f1a5 Support using reference revision as project-local= (merged =fefd2ed=) introduces project-local reference revisions — likely exactly what you want. Worth a look; may let you remove the NOTE.
- Concrete new commands from =a31f1a5=: =diff-hl-set-reference-rev-in-project= and =diff-hl-reset-reference-rev-in-project=; existing =diff-hl-reset-reference-rev= now accepts a prefix arg to wipe all per-project values. Suggested optional rebind: =gr= → =diff-hl-set-reference-rev-in-project=, =gR= → =diff-hl-reset-reference-rev-in-project=.
- Reference-revision feature substantially expanded: HEAD-vs-reference highlights now visually distinct with separate faces (=88ccf82=, =485a877=), new command =diff-hl-root-diff-reference-goto-hunk= (=5446a69=), split into a separate command from regular diff (=1678c0d=). Your existing bindings still work unchanged.
- =global-diff-hl-mode= unaffected; =diff-hl-dired-mode= gets fixes for nested paths (=73e0e62=) and simplified concurrent VC handling (=74f22fc=, =046a397=, =d0076b8=) — no config change needed.
- =diff-hl-next-hunk= / =diff-hl-previous-hunk= now support optional auto-recentering via a new option (=dbf2285=, default off); enable only if desired.
- Internal renames (=diff-hl-inline-popup= → =diff-hl-show-hunk-inline=, =4391f67=) ship with obsolete aliases (=7c57e8c=), so no breakage.
- New async modes: =359cef5= changes =diff-hl-update-async= from boolean to =nil= / =t= (new no-thread impl) / ='thread= (older Emacs). Useful on large repos / slow VC backends; default off so no behavior change for you.
- =diff-hl-fallback-to-margin= (=2cf45ee=, default =t=): on non-graphic displays auto-falls back to margin (previously fringe-only, invisible in terminals). Strict improvement.
- Other goodies: staging over Tramp (=dafd697=), new =jj= VCS support, Hg/Bzr improvements, macOS freeze fix (=08243a6=), flydiff robustness, customizable ignorable commands (=3cfd44c=), =diff-hl-dired-fringe-bmp-function= (=f5b3c3c=), =diff-hl-show-staged-changes=nil= behavior clarified (staged changes folded into reference highlights instead of hidden).

** [#B] AI analysis
*TL;DR:* Big feature/bug-fix release (v1.0.4 → v1.2.5 + ~40 main-branch commits). No breaking API changes affecting current config, but =help-mode= is now part of the default =global-colorful-modes= predicate, so the =(add-to-list 'global-colorful-modes 'help-mode)= line in =Emacs.org= is now redundant (harmless; can be removed). Also pulls in =compat-31= as a new dependency.

** Current config (=Emacs.org= ~line 5739)
#+begin_src emacs-lisp
  (use-package colorful-mode
    :config
    (add-to-list 'global-colorful-modes 'help-mode)
    (global-colorful-mode))
#+end_src

** Key change: =help-mode= now in default predicate
- =0f5986b= "Fix global-colorful-modes (github#13)" added =help-mode= to the default predicate.
- =1553fff= "Revert global-colorful-mode changes" only restored =mhtml-mode html-ts-mode latex-mode= — kept =help-mode=.
- At new tip (=97a1dc0=): predicate is ='(prog-mode help-mode html-mode css-mode latex-mode)=.
- Consequence: the =(add-to-list ... 'help-mode)= line is now redundant.

** Other notable changes (no config impact)
- v1.1.0: #RGBA / #RRGGBBAA, 0x hex colors.
- v1.2.0: CSS =@define_color= and =var()=.
- v1.2.1–1.2.3: CSS OkLab / OkLch.
- v1.2.4: switched to =jit-lock= from =font-lock-add-keywords=; =replace-region-contents=; string coloring moved into minor mode.
- v1.2.5: HSL CSS regexp fix, mouse-1 alignment fix, alpha decimals fix.
- Post-v1.2.5 (main): extensibility refactor of =colorful--colorize=, color defs moved to =colorful-colors.el=, new =colorful-add-ansi-shell-colors=, broader color conversion, =compat-31=.

** Dependency
- =compat= bumped to 31 (=3ddd228=, =97a1dc0=). Elpaca should resolve automatically.

** Recommended action
- Optional cleanup: drop the redundant =(add-to-list 'global-colorful-modes 'help-mode)=.

*TL;DR:* Nothing required. Optionally, be aware that =WIP= and =DEBUG= are now highlighted by default — if you'd rather they not be, override `hl-todo-keyword-faces`.
- User config is minimal: just `(global-hl-todo-mode)` with default `hl-todo-keyword-faces`. No breaking changes.
- User-visible: defaults now also highlight =WIP= (bfd8c3a) and =DEBUG= (9a147b9) in addition to the prior set. Comments containing these words will start getting colored.
- New flymake integration (09dc94c, 845575e): `hl-todo-flymake` / `hl-todo-make-flymake-diagnostics` — opt-in, no impact unless adopted.
- New public API: `hl-todo-syntax-table` (c13a6cf) and `hl-todo-keyword-delimiters` option (116f4e8) for customizing how keywords are delimited. Default is `'symbol`, which preserves the prior `\_<...\_>` regexp behavior — no visible change. v3.9.0 also switched the match from symbol-delimiters to symbol boundaries (f7890ab).
- Dependency: post-v3.9.3 main switched to =compat-31= (cdd8a5b).
- Rest are internal (font-lock-flush switch, regexp fixes for `hl-todo-rgrep`, build/CI, copyright bump, indentation tweaks).

** [#C] AI analysis
*TL;DR:* User config is minimal (just sets header face heights via =my/on-theme-enabled=); v2.6 → v2.8 update (74 commits) is safe to accept. A couple of default-behavior changes are worth noting but do not break the config.

- Only =markdown-mode= config is =(use-package markdown-mode ...)= at =Emacs.org=:4761 adjusting heights of =markdown-header-face-1..6=. Those faces still exist and are unchanged.
- Other mentions (=gptel-prompt-prefix-alist=, =gptel-response-prefix-alist=) only use =markdown-mode= as an alist key; nothing to migrate.
- Span: =v2.6-74-g7659bc4= → =v2.8-12-g1f72cef= (releases v2.7 and v2.8).

** Notable default-behavior changes (no action required)
- =1138d4a= =markdown-asymmetric-header= now defaults to =t=. Affects how new headings are inserted. To revert: =(setq markdown-asymmetric-header nil)=.
- =1bc4b48= =imenu-submenus-on-top= disabled by default; cosmetic ordering tweak.
- =12b39e8= =.mdx= added to =auto-mode-alist=.

** Other changes (no config impact)
- Wiki-link additions: markup hiding, dedicated faces incl. =markdown-missing-link-face=, eldoc for wiki links. Opt-in.
- D&D support (Windows / multi-drop) and =cmark= added to =markdown-command= list.
- Bugfixes: URI fontification inside inline code (=0f6ccf0=), angle URL fontification (=77cf396=), percent-decoding URLs (=2335bf5=), EOL =markdown-heading-at-point= (=0be0589=), tab-indented list bounds (=18566c2=), strike-through ordering (=c530b42=), fenced code blocks with 4+ backticks (=0525051=).
- Performance: reduced allocations in property checks (=1b97036=, =4d3dff3=).
- Some functions marked obsolete (=6f66ba3=); =360abf5= reintroduces compatibility shims. No symbol the user references is touched.
- =31eabd8= replaces =kill-this-buffer= with =kill-current-buffer= internally.
- v2.7 bumped the minimum supported Emacs version (=708fe46=).

- Internal: =a01a289= fixes return type of =string_bytes= (C module).
- *Reflow feature* (commits beyond =54c29d1=, present in some upstream tips): =995e68e= "feat: enable reflow feature from vterm 0.3+" calls =vterm_screen_enable_reflow(term->vts, true)= on every new terminal, gated by =VTermScreenEnableReflowNotExists= CMake check (older system libvterm silently skips). User-visible: long lines reflow to new width on window resize rather than being hard-wrapped/truncated; no elisp toggle. Follow-up fixes =028a2a1=/=4c07415=/=92add72= address resize/scrollback metadata corruption and remove the unused =term->resizing= flag.
- *Watch-out*: After the update the C module must rebuild via elpaca; if cmake/headers are missing vterm will be broken until fixed — open a vterm buffer post-update to confirm. Unusual scrollback wrapping after update would point at the reflow change.

** [#C] AI analysis
*TL;DR:* Nothing to do.
- Tiny update (3 commits, all from PR #91): margin-width bug fix (~342df5a~) and an internal refactor extracting window width into ~olivetti-window-width~ (~0e5d264~), merged via ~d1bdd43~.
- Specifically, =342df5a= "Do not assume that the default margin widths are zero": in =olivetti-normalize-width= and the margin-setting code, the pixel window width now adds =char-width * (left-margin-width + right-margin-width)= on top of =(window-body-width window t)=; =olivetti-reset-window= now calls =set-window-margins= with =(left-margin-width right-margin-width)= instead of =(nil nil)=, preserving buffer-local default margins on disable; the minimum allowed margin is clamped to =left-margin-width= / =right-margin-width= instead of hardcoded =0=. Improves correctness in buffers/modes that set non-zero margins.
- =0e5d264= is a pure refactor extracting =(defun olivetti-window-width (window) ...)= used in two places — no behavior change.
- User config only sets ~olivetti-body-width~ to 120 and toggles ~olivetti-mode~ via ~my/writing-mode~ (after =delete-other-windows=) — no customization of margins or window-width internals, default left/right margin widths are 0 in your buffers, so the new margin-aware path produces exactly the same result. No new/removed/renamed customs or commands.

** [#B] AI analysis
*TL;DR:* Nothing required; optionally explore the new "trim" option (`5684ef2`) if you want undo/redo to avoid adding their own undo steps.
- User config is minimal: only `(setq undo-fu-ignore-keyboard-quit t)` inside `(use-package undo-fu ...)`; `undo-fu` is used via `(setq evil-undo-system 'undo-fu)` in the evil config. No keybindings or other settings touched.
- Update is mostly bugfixes and cleanups, none of which affect the symbols the user sets:
  - `994aa7f` fixes `undo-fu-clear-all` wrongly clearing the equiv-table for all buffers (now buffer-local).
  - `c7af0da` / `d967568` / `ac67233` are internal correctness fixes (symbol comparison via `string-equal`, quoted-list handling, minor cleanups).
  - `545e294` / `4af1999` / `17fc25b` / `f78c3df` / `b4ce5ed` are docstring/readme/style cleanups only.
- The only feature change is `5684ef2`: a new "trim" option to prevent undo/redo from adding their own undo steps to the history (when redo runs it removes the undo-equiv-table entries it consumes so undo+redo pairs cancel out rather than accumulating). Opt-in via new defcustom; defaults preserve current behavior. Safe to ignore unless the user wants to try it.
